module test;
using test::*;
using system::*;

var s = "";

class SMTryCatch2 : StateMachine
{	
	$state_machine
	{
		$state_input A();
		$state_input B();

		$state ProcessA()
		{
			$switch (raise)
			{
			case A():
				{
					s = $"$(s)[A]";
				}
			}
			s = $"$(s).A";
		}

		$state ProcessB()
		{
			$switch (raise)
			{
			case B():
				{
					s = $"$(s)[B]";
				}
			}
			s = $"$(s).B";
		}
		
		$state default()
		{
			try
			{
				$push_state ProcessA();
			}
			catch (ex)
			{
				s = $"$(s)!A";
			}
			try
			{
				$push_state ProcessB();
			}
			catch (ex)
			{
				s = $"$(s)!B";
			}
			s = $"$(s).";
		}
	}
}

func main():string
{
	var sm = new SMTryCatch2^();
	try
	{
		sm.B();
		sm.A();
	}
	catch (ex)
	{
		s = $"$(s)!";
	}
	return s;
}
